                       <div class="listing__summary" data-reactid="431">
                        This is a private room, shared bath, with a queen bed, private entrance from the Main house and a part of our guesthouse Inn at Uptown Central Phoenix. There are 2 bathrooms for the 2 rooms in the main house the other rooms have their own private bathrooms. You will never bother anyone coming or going whenever you like.
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__space" data-reactid="432">
                        Cozy room with a Queen sized bed, desk and chair and a Poang reading chair. This room has a covered deck off the french doors to the back which is a great outdoor space to enjoy! This room shares a bath with the Tucson room down the hallway in between and also has access to another bathroom with a shower in the main house near the back door. Great space to combine together with the Tucson Room when traveling with more people. We have a solar heated saltwater pool which is also cooled in the summer by running the pool water at night with the system on the roof. We have a shared hot tub and lots of private places to relax and enjoy. There is a tea bar with teas and a coffee bar in the main house honor bar with self serve drinks and snacks
                       </div>
                       <div class="listing__neighborhood" data-reactid="433">
                        We are on the bike path and a wide center street between some major streets. There are 3 great restaurants in walking distance, Christos, Feeney's and Sierra Bonita. There are two convenience stores in walking distance Circle K to the East and Shell (with Deli) to the West and North only a half mile is a 24 Hour Safeway store with anything and everything. There are two Jewish Synagogues in walking distance and a Buddhist Temple.

                        This space was created with your needs in mind. It's Scandinavian simple: clean, utilitarian, bright, open, and foremost comfortable. Yeah - even the toilet paper is super. Yet, it is a historic home - from 1936 - and some of that character will shine through - plaster walls, wood windows, tall ceilings, brick exterior, funky layout and a porch are just some of the clues this home is from another century - all think you'll enjoy with while drinking French press coffee while waving to the neighbors walking their dog.
